1814:   function distKm(a,b){
1815:     const R = 6371;
1816:     const toRad = x => x * Math.PI / 180;
1817:     const dLat = toRad(Number(b.lat) - Number(a.lat));
1818:     const dLng = toRad(Number(b.lng) - Number(a.lng));
1819:     const lat1 = toRad(Number(a.lat));
1820:     const lat2 = toRad(Number(b.lat));
1821: 
1822:     const h =
1823:       Math.sin(dLat/2) * Math.sin(dLat/2) +
1824:       Math.cos(lat1) * Math.cos(lat2) *
1825:       Math.sin(dLng/2) * Math.sin(dLng/2);
1826: 
1827:     return 2 * R * Math.atan2(Math.sqrt(h), Math.sqrt(1-h));
1828:   }

35: 
36:   function distKm(a, b){
37:     const R = 6371;
38:     const toRad = d => d * Math.PI / 180;
39:     const dLat = toRad(Number(b.lat) - Number(a.lat));
40:     const dLng = toRad(Number(b.lng) - Number(a.lng));
41:     const la1 = toRad(Number(a.lat));
42:     const la2 = toRad(Number(b.lat));
43:     const h =
44:       Math.sin(dLat / 2) ** 2 +
45:       Math.cos(la1) * Math.cos(la2) * Math.sin(dLng / 2) ** 2;
46: 
47:     return 2 * R * Math.asin(Math.sqrt(h));
48:   }
49:

1808:   function formatKm(km){
1809:     if(!Number.isFinite(km) || km < 0) return "—";
1810:     if(km < 1) return Math.round(km * 1000) + " m";
1811:     return km.toFixed(2) + " km";
1812:   }
1813: 
1814:   function distKm(a,b){
1815:     const R = 6371;
1816:     const toRad = x => x * Math.PI / 180;
1817:     const dLat = toRad(Number(b.lat) - Number(a.lat));
1818:     const dLng = toRad(Number(b.lng) - Number(a.lng));
1819:     const lat1 = toRad(Number(a.lat));
1820:     const lat2 = toRad(Number(b.lat));
1821: 
1822:     const h =
1823:       Math.sin(dLat/2) * Math.sin(dLat/2) +
1824:       Math.cos(lat1) * Math.cos(lat2) *
1825:       Math.sin(dLng/2) * Math.sin(dLng/2);
1826: 
1827:     return 2 * R * Math.atan2(Math.sqrt(h), Math.sqrt(1-h));
1828:   }

[context 1946-1968]
1946:     if(!lastGpsPoint){
1947:       acceptSpeed(0);
1948:       return;
1949:     }
1950: 
1951:     const dt = Math.max(0, (point.t - lastGpsPoint.t) / 1000);
1952:     if(dt < 1 || dt > 20) return;
1953: 
1954:     const km = distKm(lastGpsPoint, point);
1955:     const meters = km * 1000;
1956: 
1957:     const acc = Number(point.accuracy || 999);
1958:     const jitterLimit = Math.max(4, Math.min(25, acc * 0.35));
1959: 
1960:     if(meters < jitterLimit){
1961:       acceptSpeed(0);
1962:       return;
1963:     }
1964: 
1965:     const kmh = km / (dt / 3600);

28:   function norm(v){
29:     return text(v)
30:       .trim()
31:       .toLocaleLowerCase("tr-TR")
32:       .replace(/[–—_\/\\.,()[\]]/g, " ")
33:       .replace(/\s+/g, " ");
34:   }
35: 
36:   function distKm(a, b){
37:     const R = 6371;
38:     const toRad = d => d * Math.PI / 180;
39:     const dLat = toRad(Number(b.lat) - Number(a.lat));
40:     const dLng = toRad(Number(b.lng) - Number(a.lng));
41:     const la1 = toRad(Number(a.lat));
42:     const la2 = toRad(Number(b.lat));
43:     const h =
44:       Math.sin(dLat / 2) ** 2 +
45:       Math.cos(la1) * Math.cos(la2) * Math.sin(dLng / 2) ** 2;
46: 
47:     return 2 * R * Math.asin(Math.sqrt(h));
48:   }
